## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task models the population growth rate dP/dt as a function of population size P and time t, which is the central problem in population dynamics. The relationship likely involves density-dependent growth mechanisms such as logistic growth, Allee effects, or time-varying carrying capacities.

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Exponential (Malthusian) growth: dP_dt = c0 * P (density-independent growth)
- Logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) (density-dependent growth with carrying capacity)
- Gompertz growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P) (growth rate decreasing logarithmically with population)
- Theta-logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (generalized logistic with shape parameter)
- Allee effect (strong): dP_dt = c0 * P * (P - c1) * (1 - c2 * P) (growth negative below threshold population)
- Allee effect (weak/cubic): dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * (1 + c2 * P) (enhanced growth at intermediate densities)
- Beverton-Holt continuous: dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (saturating per-capita growth rate)
- Logistic with harvesting: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 * P (logistic growth minus proportional removal)
- Time-varying carrying capacity: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P * (1 + c2 * sin(c3 * t))) (seasonal environmental variation)
- Richards growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (flexible sigmoid growth curve)
- Logistic with constant harvesting: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 (growth with constant yield removal)
- Power-law growth: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 (fractional-order population dynamics)
- Von Bertalanffy-type: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 - c2 * P (anabolism-catabolism balance)
- Time-dependent exponential: dP_dt = c0 * P * exp(c1 * t) (exponentially changing growth rate)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Cubic polynomial in P (terms P, P², P³) → Allee effect or bistability with two stable equilibria and one unstable equilibrium
- Product of P with a linear factor (1 - c*P) → logistic-type density dependence with a single carrying capacity
- Logarithmic dependence log(c/P) → Gompertz-type growth where per-capita rate declines logarithmically, often better for asymmetric growth curves
- Rational form P/(1+c*P) → contest competition or resource saturation where per-capita growth asymptotes rather than going negative
- Sinusoidal modulation of parameters by t → seasonal or periodic environmental forcing on birth/death rates
- Negative constant term independent of P → constant-yield harvesting or immigration/emigration at fixed rate
- Multiple roots in dP_dt as function of P → multiple equilibria indicating possible regime shifts or critical transitions
- Per-capita growth rate (dP_dt/P) decreasing linearly with P → classic logistic mechanism of intraspecific competition
